               <div class="block-title-wrap module-block-title clearfix block-title-1 with-load-more">
                <div class="block-title-area clearfix">
                 <div class="block-title font-1">
                  Neuroscience
                 </div>
                 <div class="block-subtitle font-1">
                  <p>
                   Neuroscience research articles are provided.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   What is neuroscience? Neuroscience is the scientific study of nervous systems. Neuroscience can involve research from many branches of science including those involving neurology, brain science, neurobiology, psychology, computer science, artificial intelligence, statistics, prosthetics, neuroimaging, engineering, medicine, physics, mathematics, pharmacology, electrophysiology, biology, robotics and technology.
                  </p>

               <div class="block-title-wrap module-block-title clearfix block-title-1 with-load-more">
                <div class="block-title-area clearfix">
                 <div class="block-title font-1">
                  Neurology
                 </div>
                 <div class="block-subtitle font-1">
                  <p>
                   – These articles focus mainly on neurology research.
                   <br/>
                   – What is neurology?
                   <br/>
                   – Definition of neurology: a science involved in the study of the nervous systems, especially of the diseases and disorders affecting them.
                   <br/>
                   – Neurology research can include information involving brain research, neurological disorders, medicine, brain cancer, peripheral nervous systems, central nervous systems, nerve damage, brain tumors, seizures, neurosurgery, electrophysiology, BMI, brain injuries, paralysis and spinal cord treatments.
                  </p>
                 </div>

                    The COVID-19 pandemic has had a significant impact on stress in both pregnant and postpartum women. Researchers say this is concerning as prenatal stress can hamper fetal brain development.
                    <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                     <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/covid-pregnancy-stress-18066/">
                      Read More
                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </article>

                  <div class="mask">

                    <img alt="This shows a hand holding an e cigarette" class="attachment-zeen-370-247 size-zeen-370-247 wp-post-image" height="247" sizes="(max-width: 370px) 100vw, 370px" src="https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public-370x247.jpeg" srcset="https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public-370x247.jpeg 370w, https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public-300x200.jpeg 300w, https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public-293x195.jpeg 293w, https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public-150x100.jpeg 150w, https://neurosciencenews.com/files/2021/03/vaping-schizophrenia-nerosciences-public.jpeg 770w" width="370"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="meta">
                   <div class="title-wrap">
                    <h3 class="title">
                     <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/vaping-schizophrenia-smoking-18058/">
                      Electronic Cigarettes Help Smokers With Schizophrenia Quit
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                   </div>
                   <div class="excerpt body-color">
                    Between 60-90% of people with schizophrenia smoke, compared to between 15-24% of the general population. A new study found 40% of those with schizophrenia stopped smoking traditional cigarettes after 12 weeks of switching to e-cigarettes. Researchers also reported a significant number of participants sustained their reduction in smoking or completely stopped smoking at the end of the 12-week study.
                    <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                     <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/vaping-schizophrenia-smoking-18058/">

                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </div>

                     </a>
                    </h3>
                   </div>
                   <div class="excerpt body-color">
                    Whether you are a fan of War and Peace, or would rather immerse yourself in romantic fiction, researchers say the more you read, the better your verbal skills. The study reports those who read fiction for leisure score higher on language tests than those who read to simply access specific information.

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/death-dreams-17921/">
                  As Death Approaches, Our Dreams Offer Comfort and Reconciliation
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                More than 80% of patients nearing the end of life reported experiencing dreams that were vivid, meaningful, and transformative. Patients reported the dreams made them feel supported, reassured and helped them to accept their impending death.

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/same-sex-neurobiology-17913/">
                  Differences Related to Sexual Orientation Found in the Brain
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                A new neuroimaging study reveals brain patterns that differentiate between men and women are less pronounced in non-heterosexual people. The differences occurred primarily in sensory processing areas of the brain, in particular areas associated with visual processing. Researchers say the brain differences could be linked to a genetic predisposition for same-sex sexual behaviors. The study reveals a neurobiological basis for same-sex attractions.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/same-sex-neurobiology-17913/">
                  Read More
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/gut-microbes-neurodevelopment-18008/">
                  Gut Microbes May Hold the Key for Treating Neurological Disorders
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                In mouse models of neurodevelopmental disorders, researchers found social deficits were mediated by microbes in the gut. By contrast, hyperactivity is controlled by genetics. Treatment with a specific microbe helped improve social behavior.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/gut-microbes-neurodevelopment-18008/">

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/cardiomyocytes-heart-energy-drinks-17730/">
                  Energy Drinks’ Harmful Effects on Heart
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                Exposure to energy drinks increases heart rate and impacts cardiovascular function, researchers report. Energy drinks may have a significant impact on human cardiomyocytes.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/cardiomyocytes-heart-energy-drinks-17730/">

                 </a>

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/behavior-psychosis-pathway-17834/">
                  Neural Pathway Critical to Correcting Behavioral Errors in Psychiatric Disorders Identified
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                Study identifies a neural pathway associated with error monitoring and attention function in some psychiatric disorders such as ADHD, ASD, and schizophrenia. Researchers say the pathway could be modulated with the help of transcranial magnetic stimulation or transcranial direct current stimulation.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/behavior-psychosis-pathway-17834/">
                  Read More
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/proprioception-neuroscience-17839/">
                  Proprioception, Our Imperceptible 6th Sense
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                Proprioception allows us to determine the position, speed, and direction of each of our body parts, and enables our brains to guide our movements. Researchers explore what happens in the brain when proprioception is lost.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/proprioception-neuroscience-17839/">
                  Read More
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>

               <div class="title-wrap">
                <h3 class="title">
                 <a href="https://neurosciencenews.com/hand-writing-brain-activity-18069/">
                  Stronger Brain Activity After Writing on Paper Than on Tablet or Smartphone
                 </a>
                </h3>
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt body-color">
                Writing by hand increases brain activity in recall tasks over taking notes on a tablet or smartphone. Additionally, those who write by hand on paper are 25% quicker at note-taking tasks than those who use digital technology.
                <span class="read-more-wrap font-3">
                 <a class="read-more tipi-button custom-button__fill-1 custom-button__rounded-1" href="https://neurosciencenews.com/hand-writing-brain-activity-18069/">
                  Read More
                 </a>
